When you stop the function clicking on \"Stop follow me\", the route will not be stored in the device. This way, if you go from point B to point A, you can follow a route on map previously stored and loaded (follow back).\r\n\r\n4) Replay route on the map (a route previously stored in step 2). All colors, small images and icons will be converted to give you the smoothest dark experience possible.\r\n\r\n- Filtered - The websites' colors will not be changed, but you can still adjust brightness, contrast, warmth and more.\r\n\r\n- Normal - Get back to the normal browsing experience.\r\n\r\n\r\nAny modifications you make such as contrast level adjustment, colors and etc. can be applied to a single website or globally.\r\n\r\nNew features:\r\n- Scheduled on/off\r\n- Updated color picker\r\n\r\n \r\nBuilt-in support system - we take pride into being available to provide reliable support and help you with any problems or issues you might experience with the extension.\r\n\r\n\r\nNight Eye is currently working on Microsoft Edge, Google Chrome, Mozilla Firefox, Opera, Vivaldi, and Yandex web browsers.
